within the source files using Markdown. cargo doc can then generate beautiful HTML documentation from this. If we have larger
 Markdown files explaining specific Rust crates or modules, we can use #[doc = include_str!("../path/to/your_doc.md")] within
 the lib.rs or main.rs of that crate. This effectively "includes" the external Markdown file into the crate's generated
documentation, making it part of the "cargo manifest" in a functional sense.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Cargo.toml</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">documentation</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> field: The [package] section in Cargo.toml has a documentation field where we can point to a
hosted documentation website (e.g., on docs.rs or GitHub Pages).</span></span></span></li></ol><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">  For our current task of documenting </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">solfunmeme_clifford</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> and its users:</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">  I will continue with the plan to identify which Cargo.toml files depend on solfunmeme_clifford.  â”‚     1 # Sophia RDF Library Integration SOP                                                                                      â”‚
 â”‚     2                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚     3 This document outlines the standard operating procedures for integrating and utilizing the </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sophia</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> RDF                   â”‚
 â”‚       library within the </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">ragit</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> project.                                                                                       â”‚
 â”‚     4                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚     5 ## 1. High-Level Strategy                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     6                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚     7 The core strategy for using </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sophia</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> is to abstract its complexities behind a dedicated wrapper crate:                    â”‚
 â”‚       </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">solfunmeme_rdf_utils</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">. This approach provides a simplified, high-level API for common RDF operations,                    â”‚
 â”‚       reducing boilerplate code and isolating the rest of the codebase from direct dependencies on </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sophia</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">. This is            â”‚
 â”‚       crucial for managing the complexity of the </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sophia</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> API and for mitigating the impact of breaking changes in              â”‚
 â”‚       future versions.                                                                                                          â”‚
 â”‚     8                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚     9 ## 2. Core Functionality                                                                                                  â”‚
 â”‚    10                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    11 </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sophia</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> is primarily used for the following RDF-related tasks:                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    12                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    13 *   </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**Parsing:**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> Parsing Turtle (</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">.ttl</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">) and other RDF formats into in-memory graph structures.                           â”‚
 â”‚    14 *   </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**Querying:**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> Programmatically querying the RDF graphs to retrieve semantic data.                                     â”‚
 â”‚    15 *   </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**Serialization:**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> Serializing in-memory graphs back into Turtle (</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">.ttl</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">) files.                                      â”‚
 â”‚    16 *   </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**Graph Manipulation:**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> Creating, updating, and managing RDF graphs.                                                  â”‚
 â”‚    17                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    18 ## 3. Key Crates and Modules                                                                                              â”‚
 â”‚    19                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    20 The following crates and modules are central to the </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sophia</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> integration:                                                 â”‚
 â”‚    21                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    22 *   </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**`solfunmeme_rdf_utils`:**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> The primary wrapper crate for </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sophia</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">. All new code that needs to interact               â”‚
 â”‚       with RDF data should use the utilities provided by this crate.                                                            â”‚
 â”‚    23 *   </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**`solfunmeme_core_logic`:**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> Directly uses </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sophia</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> for RDF graph manipulation.                                       â”‚
 â”‚    24 *   </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**`prepare_sources`:**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> The </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">ontology_generator</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> module within this crate uses </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sophia</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> to create RDF                  â”‚
 â”‚       ontologies from analyzed function data.                                                                                   â”‚
 â”‚    25 *   </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**`task_manager`:**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> Uses </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sophia</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> for parsing, querying, and updating the task graph.                                 â”‚
 â”‚    26 *   </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**`jsonld_plugin`:**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> Uses </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sophia_jsonld</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> for JSON-LD processing.                                                     â”‚
 â”‚    27                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    28 ## 4. Sophia 0.8 Migration                                                                                                â”‚
 â”‚    29                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    30 The migration from </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sophia</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> version 0.7 to 0.8 introduced significant breaking changes due to the adoption of             â”‚
 â”‚       Generic Associated Types (GATs). Key points to remember when working with </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sophia</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> 0.8.0+ are:                            â”‚
 â”‚    31                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    32 *   </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**Term and IRI Types:**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> The </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">TTerm</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> trait has been replaced by the new </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Term</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> trait. IRI-related types are            â”‚
 â”‚       now primarily located in the </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sophia_iri</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> crate.                                                                          â”‚
 â”‚    33 *   </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**Graph Methods:**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> Methods like </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">triples_with_s</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> have been replaced by the more general </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">triples_matching</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">            â”‚
 â”‚       method.                                                                                                                   â”‚
 â”‚    34 *   </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**Serializer Traits:**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> When using serializers like </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">TurtleSerializer</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">, ensure that the                                â”‚
 â”‚       </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sophia_api::prefix::PrefixSink</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> and </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sophia_api::serializer::StreamSerializer</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> traits are in scope.                      â”‚
 â”‚    35 *   </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**Owned vs. Borrowed Types:**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> Be mindful of Rust's ownership and borrowing rules, especially when                     â”‚
 â”‚       converting between </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">&amp;str</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> and </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">String</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> for </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Term</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> types.                                                                  â”‚
 â”‚    36                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    37 ## 5. Code Examples                                                                                                       â”‚

 â”‚    76 ## 6. Conclusion                                                                                                          â”‚
 â”‚    77                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    78 By adhering to these procedures, we can ensure a consistent and maintainable integration of the </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sophia</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> RDF              â”‚
 â”‚       library, enabling powerful semantic data capabilities within the </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">ragit</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> project.                                         â”‚

 â”‚    13 *   </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**`solfunmeme_rdf_utils`**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: This crate acts as a wrapper around the </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sophia</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> RDF library, providing core              â”‚
 â”‚       functionalities for RDF graph manipulation, including loading from files, merging graphs, and serializing to              â”‚
 â”‚       Turtle format. </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">solfunmeme_ontology_vibe</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> extensively uses </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">solfunmeme_rdf_utils::rdf_graph::RdfGraph</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> for all            â”‚
 â”‚       its RDF operations.                                                                                                       â”‚
 â”‚    14 *   </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**`solfunmeme_clifford`**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: This crate is responsible for generating Clifford multivectors from string                 â”‚
 â”‚       inputs. These multivectors are used to semantically enrich the ontology data, particularly for representing               â”‚
 â”‚       crate names and emojis.                                                                                                   â”‚
 â”‚    15                                                                                                                           â”‚

 â”‚    22 </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**Purpose**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Responsible for loading RDF graphs from Turtle (</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">.ttl</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">) files.                                               â”‚

 â”‚    28 *   Returns a combined </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">RdfGraph</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> instance.                                                                               â”‚
 â”‚    29                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    30 </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**Usage Example (from `lib.rs`):**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">                                                                                        â”‚

 â”‚    38 ### </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">processor</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> Module                                                                                                    â”‚

 â”‚    40 </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**Purpose**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Responsible for processing the loaded RDF graph, specifically by adding semantic data (Clifford              â”‚

 â”‚    42 </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**Sub-modules**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:                                                                                                          â”‚
 â”‚    43                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    44 *   </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**`crate_data`**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Adds multivector representations for crate data.                                                    â”‚
 â”‚    45     *   </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**Key Function**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">add_crate_data_internal(graph: &amp;mut RdfGraph)</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">                                                 â”‚
 â”‚    46     *   Identifies subjects in the graph that are of type </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">rdfs:Class</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> and have a </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">rdfs:label</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> property,                  â”‚
 â”‚       particularly those prefixed with </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">crates_root</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">.                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    47     *   Generates a Clifford multivector from the crate's label using                                                     â”‚
 â”‚       </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">solfunmeme_clifford::generate_multivector_from_string</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">.                                                                  â”‚
 â”‚    48     *   Adds a new triple to the graph, linking the crate subject to its multivector representation using the             â”‚
 â”‚       </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">onto:hasCliffordVector</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> property.                                                                                        â”‚
 â”‚    49                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    50 *   </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**`emoji_data`**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Adds multivector representations for emoji data.                                                    â”‚
 â”‚    51     *   </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**Key Function**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">add_emoji_data_internal(graph: &amp;mut RdfGraph)</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">                                                 â”‚
 â”‚    52     *   Identifies subjects in the graph that are of type </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">em:Emoji</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">.                                                     â”‚
 â”‚    53     *   Generates a Clifford multivector from the emoji's name (extracted from its IRI) using                             â”‚
 â”‚       </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">solfunmeme_clifford::generate_multivector_from_string</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">.                                                                  â”‚
 â”‚    54     *   Adds a new triple to the graph, linking the emoji subject to its multivector representation using the             â”‚
 â”‚       </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">onto:hasCliffordVector</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> property.                                                                                        â”‚
 â”‚    55                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    56 </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**Usage Examples (from `lib.rs`):**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">                                                                                       â”‚
 â”‚    57                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    58 </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">rust                                                                                                                   â”‚  â”‚    59 pub fn add_crate_data(graph: &amp;mut RdfGraph) -&gt; Result&lt;()&gt; {                                                               â”‚  â”‚    60     processor::crate_data::add_crate_data_internal(graph)                                                                 â”‚  â”‚    61 }                                                                                                                         â”‚  â”‚    62                                                                                                                           â”‚  â”‚    63 pub fn add_emoji_data(graph: &amp;mut RdfGraph) -&gt; Result&lt;()&gt; {                                                               â”‚  â”‚    64     processor::emoji_data::add_emoji_data_internal(graph)                                                                 â”‚  â”‚    65 }                                                                                                                         â”‚  â”‚    66 </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">                                                                                                                       â”‚
 â”‚    67                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    68 ### </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">serializer</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> Module                                                                                                   â”‚
 â”‚    69                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    70 </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**Purpose**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Responsible for serializing the processed RDF graph back into a Turtle (</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">.ttl</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">) file.                        â”‚
 â”‚    71                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    72 </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**Key Function**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">serialize_graph_internal(graph: &amp;RdfGraph)</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">                                                            â”‚
 â”‚    73                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    74 *   Serializes the provided </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">RdfGraph</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> instance to </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">ontologies/index.ttl</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">.                                                â”‚
 â”‚    75 *   Leverages </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">solfunmeme_rdf_utils::rdf_graph::RdfGraph::serialize_to_turtle</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> for the serialization process.             â”‚
 â”‚    76                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    77 </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">**Usage Example (from `lib.rs`):**</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">                                                                                        â”‚
 â”‚    78                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    79 </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">rust                                                                                                                   â”‚  â”‚    80 pub fn serialize_graph(graph: &amp;RdfGraph) -&gt; Result&lt;()&gt; {                                                                  â”‚  â”‚    81     serializer::serialize_graph_internal(graph)                                                                           â”‚  â”‚    82 }                                                                                                                         â”‚  â”‚    83 </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">                                                                                                                       â”‚
 â”‚    84                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    85 ## Interaction with </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">solfunmeme_rdf_utils</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> and </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">solfunmeme_clifford</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">                                                      â”‚
 â”‚    86                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    87 </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">solfunmeme_ontology_vibe</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> acts as an orchestrator, utilizing the functionalities provided by its                         â”‚
 â”‚       dependencies:                                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚    88                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    89 *   It relies on </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">solfunmeme_rdf_utils</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> for all low-level RDF operations, such as file I/O for Turtle files,              â”‚
 â”‚       graph merging, and adding triples. This ensures that the complexities of </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">sophia</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> are contained within                    â”‚
 â”‚       </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">solfunmeme_rdf_utils</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">.                                                                                                   â”‚
 â”‚    90 *   It uses </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">solfunmeme_clifford</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> to generate semantic representations (multivectors) for various entities                â”‚
 â”‚       (crates, emojis) within the ontology. These multivectors are then integrated into the RDF graph as literal                â”‚
 â”‚       triples.                                                                                                                  â”‚
 â”‚    91                                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚    92 This layered approach allows </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">solfunmeme_ontology_vibe</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> to focus on the domain-specific logic of ontology                 â”‚
 â”‚       management, while delegating the generic RDF and Clifford algebra operations to its specialized dependencies.             â”‚

3 use solfunmeme_rdf_utils::rdf_graph::RdfGraph;
4 use sophia_api::term::{SimpleTerm, Term};
5 use sophia_api::iri::Iri;

7 fn main() -&gt; Result&lt;()&gt; {

9     let mut graph = load_graph()?;</span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">   10     println!("Graph loaded successfully.");

   14     let my_new_class_iri = Iri::new("</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">http://example.org/MyNewClass</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">")?;
   15     let rdf_type_iri = Iri::new("</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#type</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">")?;
   16     let rdfs_class_iri = Iri::new("</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#Class</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">")?;
   17
   18     graph.add_triple(
   19         &amp;SimpleTerm::Iri(my_new_class_iri.clone()),
   20         &amp;SimpleTerm::Iri(rdf_type_iri.clone()),
   21         &amp;SimpleTerm::Iri(rdfs_class_iri.clone()),
   22     )?;
   23     println!("Added new class: MyNewClass");
   24
   25     // Example: Adding a new property "hasAttribute"
   26     let has_attribute_iri = Iri::new("</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">http://example.org/hasAttribute</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">")?;
   27     let rdf_property_iri = Iri::new("</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#Property</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">")?;
   28
   29     graph.add_triple(
   30         &amp;SimpleTerm::Iri(has_attribute_iri.clone()),
   31         &amp;SimpleTerm::Iri(rdf_type_iri.clone()),
   32         &amp;SimpleTerm::Iri(rdf_property_iri.clone()),
   33     )?;
   34     println!("Added new property: hasAttribute");
   35
   36     // Example: Adding an instance of MyNewClass with an attribute
   37     let my_instance_iri = Iri::new("</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">http://example.org/myInstance</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">")?;
   38     let literal_value = SimpleTerm::Literal("some value".to_string(), None, None);
   39
   40     graph.add_triple(
   41         &amp;SimpleTerm::Iri(my_instance_iri.clone()),
   42         &amp;SimpleTerm::Iri(rdf_type_iri.clone()),
   43         &amp;SimpleTerm::Iri(my_new_class_iri.clone()),
   44     )?;
   45     graph.add_triple(
   46         &amp;SimpleTerm::Iri(my_instance_iri.clone()),
   47         &amp;SimpleTerm::Iri(has_attribute_iri.clone()),
   48         &amp;literal_value,
   49     )?;
   50     println!("Added new instance: myInstance with an attribute.");
   51
   52     // 3. Serialize the updated graph back to the file
   53     serialize_graph(&amp;graph)?;
   54     println!("Graph serialized successfully to ontologies/index.ttl.");
   55
   56     Ok(())
   57 }</span></span></span></span><ol dir="ltr" start="3" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Update </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">crates/layer7_application/add_custom_term/Cargo.toml</span></span></span></li></ol><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">  You'll need to create a Cargo.toml for this new binary, ensuring it depends on solfunmeme_ontology_vibe and solfunmeme_rdf_utils.</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">1 [package]

  "Programmatic Code Transformation" philosophy.</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">â•­â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â•®

  happening.

margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Commit these changes.</span></span></span></li></ol><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">  Let's proceed with creating the documentation for solfunmeme_clifford.</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">â„¹ Request cancelled.</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">âœ• [API Error: Cannot read properties of undefined (reading 'error')]</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">â•­â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â•®

I’ll also ensure documentation is discoverable by leveraging Rust’s conventions.</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; margin-top: 1.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Creating </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">docs/rust_code/solfunmeme_clifford.md</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Here’s the proposed content for the documentation:</span></span></span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-1adg3ll r-ag158w r-dnmrzs r-1yx7oqi r-13qz1uu"><div class="css-175oi2r r-dnmrzs r-1adg3ll r-13qz1uu" data-testid="markdown-code-block"><div class="css-175oi2r r-1awozwy r-1fkb3t2 r-1fs5b29 r-1idry7j r-6413gk r-43g30s r-l4nmg1 r-1u658rm r-2dysd3 r-vmopo1 r-13qz1uu r-gtdqiz r-1fhadnw r-184en5c"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-1aiqnjv r-n6v787"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">markdown</span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-xoduu5 r-1ybcz0z"></div></div><pre style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.3; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; padding: 12px; margin: 0px 0px 0.5em; overflow: auto; background: rgb(22, 24, 28); display: block; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; border-bottom-left-radius: 8px; border-bottom-right-radius: 8px;"><code class="language-markdown" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.5; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none;"><span class="token title" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">#</span><span class="token title" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"> `solfunmeme_clifford` Crate Documentation</span><span>
</span>
<span>This document provides an overview of the </span><span class="token code-snippet code" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">`solfunmeme_clifford`</span><span> Rust crate, detailing its purpose, structure, and interactions within the Solfunmeme-Dioxus project.
</span>
<span></span><span class="token title" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">##</span><span class="token title" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"> Overview</span><span>
</span>
<span>The </span><span class="token code-snippet code" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">`solfunmeme_clifford`</span><span> crate implements a 3D Clifford algebra for generating and manipulating multivectors, which are used to create semantic representations of data (e.g., crate names, emojis) in the Solfunmeme-Dioxus project. These multivectors are integrated into RDF graphs via the </span><span class="token code-snippet code" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">`solfunmeme_ontology_vibe`</span><span> crate to enrich ontology data with geometric algebra-based semantics.
</span>
<span></span><span class="token title" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">##</span><span class="token title" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"> Dependencies</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token code-snippet code" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">`solfunmeme_clifford`</span><span> depends on the following crates:
</span><span></span><span class="token list" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> </span><span class="token bold" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">**</span><span class="token bold content code-snippet code">`tclifford`</span><span class="token bold" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">**</span><span>: Provides the underlying Clifford algebra implementation.
</span><span></span><span class="token list" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> </span><span class="token bold" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">**</span><span class="token bold content code-snippet code">`rand`</span><span class="token bold" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">**</span><span>: Used for generating random coefficients in some multivector operations.
</span><span></span><span class="token list" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> </span><span class="token bold" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">**</span><span class="token bold content code-snippet code">`serde`</span><span class="token bold" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">**</span><span>: Enables serialization and deserialization of multivectors.
</span><span></span><span class="token list" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> </span><span class="token bold" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">**</span><span class="token bold content code-snippet code">`anyhow`</span><span class="token bold" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">**</span><span>: Simplifies error handling.
</span><span></span><span class="token list" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> </span><span class="token bold" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">**</span><span class="token bold content code-snippet code">`sha2`</span><span class="token bold" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">**</span><span>: Provides SHA-256 hashing for converting strings to multivectors.
</span>
<span></span><span class="token title" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">##</span><span class="token title" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"> Core Functionality</span><span>
</span>
The crate defines the following key components:

<span></span><span class="token title" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">###</span><span class="token title" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"> `SolCliffordAlgebra`</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token list" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> Represents a 3D Clifford algebra with basis vectors (e.g., e0, e1, e2).
</span><span></span><span class="token list" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> Provides operations for geometric products, outer products, and other algebraic manipulations.
</span>
<span></span><span class="token title" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">###</span><span class="token title" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"> `SolMultivector`</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token list" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> A struct representing a multivector in the 3D Clifford algebra.
</span><span></span><span class="token list" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> Contains coefficients for scalar, vector, bivector, and trivector components.
</span><span></span><span class="token list" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> Key methods:
</span><span>  </span><span class="token list" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> </span><span class="token code-snippet code" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">`get_multivector_norm`</span><span>: Computes the norm (magnitude) of the multivector.
</span><span>  </span><span class="token list" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> </span><span class="token code-snippet code" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">`get_multivector_coefficients`</span><span>: Returns the coefficients of the multivector's basis components.
</span>
<span></span><span class="token title" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">###</span><span class="token title" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"> `generate_multivector_from_string`</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token list" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> </span><span class="token bold" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">**</span><span class="token bold content">Signature</span><span class="token bold" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">**</span><span>: </span><span class="token code-snippet code" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">`fn generate_multivector_from_string(input: &amp;str) -&gt; Result&lt;SolMultivector&gt;`</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token list" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> Converts a string input (e.g., a crate name or emoji) into a </span><span class="token code-snippet code" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">`SolMultivector`</span><span> using SHA-256 hashing.
</span><span></span><span class="token list" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> The hash is used to derive deterministic coefficients for the multivector’s basis components, ensuring consistent semantic representations.
</span>
<span></span><span class="token title" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">###</span><span class="token title" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"> `SerializableMultivector`</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token list" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> A struct for serializing and deserializing </span><span class="token code-snippet code" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">`SolMultivector`</span><span> instances.
</span><span></span><span class="token list" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> Uses </span><span class="token code-snippet code" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">`serde`</span><span> to convert multivectors to/from formats like JSON or Turtle (when integrated with RDF).
</span>
<span></span><span class="token title" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">##</span><span class="token title" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"> Usage in Solfunmeme-Dioxus</span><span>
</span>
<span></span><span class="token code-snippet code" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">`solfunmeme_clifford`</span><span> is primarily used by the </span><span class="token code-snippet code" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">`solfunmeme_ontology_vibe`</span><span> crate, specifically in:
</span><span></span><span class="token list" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> </span><span class="token code-snippet code" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">`processor/crate_data.rs`</span><span>: Generates multivectors for crate names and adds them as </span><span class="token code-snippet code" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">`onto:hasCliffordVector`</span><span> triples to the RDF graph.
</span><span></span><span class="token list" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-</span><span> </span><span class="token code-snippet code" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">`processor/emoji_data.rs`</span><span>: Generates multivectors for emoji names and adds them as </span><span class="token code-snippet code" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">`onto:hasCliffordVector`</span><span> triples.
</span>
<span>Example usage (from </span><span class="token code-snippet code" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">`solfunmeme_ontology_vibe`</span><span>):
</span>```rust
use solfunmeme_clifford::generate_multivector_from_string;
use solfunmeme_rdf_utils::rdf_graph::RdfGraph;

<span>fn add_crate_data_internal(graph: &amp;mut RdfGraph) -&gt; Result</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(128, 128, 128);">&lt;</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">()</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(128, 128, 128);">&gt;</span><span> {
</span>    // Example: For each crate subject with rdfs:label
    let crate_name = "example_crate";
    let multivector = generate_multivector_from_string(crate_name)?;
    // Add multivector as a literal triple to the RDF graph
    // ...
    Ok(())
}</code></pre></div></div><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1blvdjr r-vrz42v r-b88u0q" style="display: block; margin-top: 1.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Integration with Other Crates</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">solfunmeme_clifford</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> is a dependency for multiple crates in the Solfunmeme-Dioxus project (15 Cargo.toml files reference it). This might involve a library like </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">rust-bert</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> or a custom implementation.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Convert to Multivector</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Modify or extend </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">solfunmeme_clifford::generate_multivector_from_string</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> to accept a BERT embedding (a float vector) and map it to a </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">SolMultivector</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">.
